     6	# Clear the output file if it exists
     7	> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
     8	
     9	# Add header with date
    10	echo "MERN Project Analysis" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    11	echo "Generated on: $(date)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    12	echo "==================================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    13	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    14	
    15	# Section 1: Directory Structure
    16	echo "Section 1: Directory Structure" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    17	echo "-----------------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    18	# Exclude both node_modules and .git
    19	tree -I "node_modules|.git" --noreport . >> "$OUTPUT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo "Tree command failed (install with 'sudo apt install tree' or equivalent)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    20	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    21	
    22	# Section 2: File Details
    23	echo "Section 2: File Details" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    24	echo "----------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    25	# Exclude both node_modules and .git in find
    26	find . -type f -not -path "*/node_modules/*" -not -path "*/.git/*" | sort | while read -r file; do
    27	    echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    28	    echo "Size: $(stat -c %s "$file") bytes" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    29	    echo "Permissions: $(stat -c %A "$file")" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    30	    echo "Last Modified: $(stat -c %y "$file")" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    31	    echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    32	done
    33	
    34	# Section 3: File Contents
    35	echo "Section 3: File Contents" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    36	echo "-----------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    37	find . -type f -not -path "*/node_modules/*" -not -path "*/.git/*" | sort | while read -r file; do
    38	    # Skip binary files and common non-code files
    39	    if [[ ! $file =~ \.(png|jpg|jpeg|gif|svg|ico|pdf|bin|zip|tar|gz)$ ]]; then
    40	        echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    41	        echo "----------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    42	        # Add file content with line numbers, handle errors silently
    43	        cat -n "$file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo "Unable to read file contents" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    44	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    45	        echo "=================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    46	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    47	    else
    48	        echo "File: $file" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    49	        echo "----------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    50	        echo "(Binary file - contents not displayed)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    51	        echo "=================" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    52	        echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    53	    fi
    54	done
    55	
    56	# Section 4: Project Summary
    57	echo "Section 4: Project Summary" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    58	echo "-------------------------" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    59	echo "Total Directories: $(find . -type d -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' | wc -l)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    60	echo "Total Files: $(find . -type f -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' | wc -l)" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    61	echo "Total Size: $(find . -type f -not -path '*/node_modules/*' -not -path '*/.git/*' -exec stat -c %s {} \; | awk '{sum += $1} END {print sum}') bytes" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    62	echo "" >> "$OUTPUT_FILE"
    63	
    64	echo "Project analysis complete. Results saved in $OUTPUT_FILE"
=================

File: ./backend/config/db.js
----------------
     1	const mongoose = require('mongoose');
     2	const connectDB = async () => {
     3	  let retries = 5;
     4	  while (retries) {
     5	    try {
     6	      await mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGO_URI, {});
     7	      console.log('MongoDB connected');
     8	      break;
     9	    } catch (error) {
    10	      console.error('MongoDB connection error:', error);
    11	      retries--;
    12	      if (!retries) process.exit(1);
    13	      await new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, 5000));
    14	    }
    15	  }
    16	};
    17	module.exports = connectDB;

File: ./backend/middleware/auth.js
----------------
     1	const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
     2	
     3	const auth = (req, res, next) => {
     4	  const token = req.header('Authorization');
     5	  if (!token) return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'No token provided' });
     6	
     7	  try {
     8	    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
     9	    req.user = decoded; // { id: userId }
    10	    next();
    11	  } catch (error) {
    12	    res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Invalid token' });
    13	  }
    14	};
    15	
    16	module.exports = auth;
=================

File: ./backend/models/Availability.js
----------------
     1	const mongoose = require('mongoose');
     2	
     3	const timeSlotSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
     4	  start: {
     5	    type: String, 
     6	    required: true,
     7	  },
     8	  end: {
     9	    type: String, 
    10	    required: true,
    11	  },
    12	});
    13	
    14	const daySchema = new mongoose.Schema({
    15	  checked: {
    16	    type: Boolean,
    17	    default: false,
    18	  },
    19	  times: [timeSlotSchema], 
    20	});
    21	
    22	const availabilitySchema = new mongoose.Schema({
    23	  user: {
    24	    type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId,
    25	    ref: 'User',
    26	    required: true,
    27	    unique: true,
    28	  },
    29	  days: {
    30	    Sun: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: false, times: [] } },
    31	    Mon: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    32	    Tue: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    33	    Wed: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    34	    Thu: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    35	    Fri: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    36	    Sat: { type: daySchema, default: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '09:00', end: '17:00' }] } },
    37	  },
    38	  timeZone: {
    39	    type: String,
    40	    default: 'India Standard Time',
    41	  },
    42	}, { timestamps: true });
    43	
    44	module.exports = mongoose.model('Availability', availabilitySchema);

File: ./backend/routes/auth.js
----------------
     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
     4	const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
     5	const User = require('../models/User');
     6	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     7	
     8	// Signup
     9	router.post('/signup', async (req, res) => {
    10	  const {firstName, lastName, username=null, email, password } = req.body;
    11	  // console.log(username)
    12	  try {
    13	    if (!email || !password) {
    14	      return res.status(400).json({ success:false, message: 'All fields are required' });
    15	    }
    16	    const existingUser = await User.findOne({ email });
    17	    if (existingUser) {
    18	      return res.status(409).json({ success:false, message: 'User already exists' });
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    const hashedPass = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    22	
    23	    const user = new User({ firstName, lastName, email, password: hashedPass });
    24	    await user.save();
    25	    res.status(201).json({success:true, message: 'User created' });
    26	  } catch (error) {
    27	    res.status(500).json({ success:false, error: error.message });
    28	  }
    29	});
    30	
    31	// Login
    32	router.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
    33	  const { email, password } = req.body;
    34	  try {
    35	    const user = await User.findOne({ email });
    36	    if (!user || !(await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password))) {
    37	      return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: 'Invalid credentials' });
    38	    }
    39	    const token = jwt.sign({ id: user._id }, process.env.JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '4h' });
    40	    const name = user.firstName+' '+user.lastName;
    41	    res.json({ token, user:{ id: user._id, name } , success:true, message: "User Logged in successfully"});
    42	  } catch (error) {
    43	    res.status(500).json({success:false, error: error.message });
    44	  }
    45	});
    46	
    47	// Get Profile
    48	router.get('/profile', auth, async (req, res) => {
    49	  try {
    50	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    51	    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({success:false, error: 'User not found' });
    52	    res.json({success:true, user});
    53	  } catch (error) {
    54	    res.status(500).json({ success:false, error: error.message });
    55	  }
    56	});
    57	
    58	// Update Profile (with logout on email/password change)
    59	router.put('/profile', auth, async (req, res) => {
    60	  const { firstName, lastName, username , email, password } = req.body;
    61	  try {
    62	    const user = await User.findById(req.user.id);
    63	    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ success:false, error: 'User not found' });
    64	
    65	    let shouldLogout = false;
    66	    if (username) user.username = username;
    67	    if (firstName) user.firstName = firstName;
    68	    if (lastName) user.lastName = lastName;
    69	    if (email && email !== user.email) {
    70	      user.email = email;
    71	      shouldLogout = true;
    72	    }
    73	    const hashedPass = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    74	    if (password) {
    75	      user.password = hashedPass;
    76	      shouldLogout = true;
    77	    }
    78	    user.updatedAt = Date.now();
    79	    await user.save();
    80	
    81	    res.json({ success: true, message: 'Profile updated', shouldLogout });
    82	  } catch (error) {
    83	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
    84	  }
    85	});
    86	
    87	module.exports = router;

File: ./backend/routes/availability.js
----------------
     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const Availability = require('../models/Availability');
     4	const auth = require('../middleware/auth');
     5	
     6	// Get Availability
     7	router.get('/', auth, async (req, res) => {
     8	  try {
     9	    let availability = await Availability.findOne({ user: req.user.id });
    10	    if(!availability){
    11	      availability = new Availability({
    12	        user : req.user.id,
    13	        days: {
    14	          Sun: { checked: false, times: [] },
    15	          Mon: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    16	          Tue: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    17	          Wed: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    18	          Thu: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    19	          Fri: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    20	          Sat: { checked: true, times: [{ start: '00:00', end: '23:59' }] },
    21	        },
    22	        timeZone: 'India Standard Time',
    23	      })
    24	      await availability.save();
    25	    }
    26	    res.json({ success: true, availability });
    27	  } catch (error) {
    28	    console.error(error);
    29	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Server error' });
    30	  }
    31	});
    32	
    33	//put to update the availability
    34	router.put('/', auth, async(req, res) => {
    35	  try{
    36	    const { days, timeZone } = req.body;
    37	    
    38	    //vallidatios apply
    39	    if (!days || typeof days !== 'object') {
    40	      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid days data' });
    41	    }
    42	    
    43	    let availability = await Availability.findOne({ user: req.user.id });
    44	
    45	    if (!availability) {
    46	      availability = new Availability({
    47	        user: req.user.id,
    48	        days,
    49	        timeZone: timeZone || 'India Standard Time',
    50	      });
    51	    } else {
    52	      availability.days = days;
    53	      if (timeZone) availability.timeZone = timeZone;
    54	    }
    55	    await availability.save();
    56	    res.json({ success: true, availability });
    57	  }
    58	  catch(error){
    59	    console.error(error);
    60	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Server error' });
    61	  }
    62	})
    63	
    64	module.exports = router;

File: ./backend/routes/events.js
----------------
     1	const express = require("express");
     2	const router = express.Router();
     3	const Event = require("../models/Event");
     4	const Availability = require("../models/Availability");
     5	const auth = require("../middleware/auth");
     6	const bcrypt = require("bcryptjs");
     7	const User = require("../models/User");
     8	const mongoose = require("mongoose");
     9	
    10	// Create Event
    11	router.post("/", auth, async (req, res) => {
    12	  const {
    13	    title,
    14	    description,
    15	    dateTime,
    16	    duration,
    17	    link,
    18	    bannerText,
    19	    backgroundColor,
    20	    password,
    21	    emails,
    22	  } = req.body;
    23	
    24	  try {
    25	    // Convert event times to Date objects
    26	    const eventStart = new Date(dateTime); 
    27	    const eventEnd = new Date(eventStart.getTime() + duration * 60000);
    28	
    29	    const dayOfWeek = ["Sun", "Mon", "Tue", "Wed", "Thu", "Fri", "Sat"][eventStart.getDay()];
    30	    const eventStartTime = eventStart.toTimeString().slice(0, 5);
    31	    const eventEndTime = eventEnd.toTimeString().slice(0, 5);
    32	
    33	    const availability = await Availability.findOne({ user: req.user.id });
    34	    if (!availability) {
    35	      return res
    36	        .status(404)
    37	        .json({ success: false, error: "No availability set for this user" });
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    const dayAvailability = availability.days[dayOfWeek];
    41	    if (!dayAvailability.checked) {
    42	      return res
    43	        .status(409)
    44	        .json({ success: false, error: `Not available on ${dayOfWeek}` });
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    const isAvailable = dayAvailability.times.some((slot) => {
    48	      const slotStart = slot.start;
    49	      const slotEnd = slot.end;
    50	      
    51	      return slotStart <= eventStartTime && slotEnd >= eventEndTime;
    52	    });
    53	
    54	    if (!isAvailable) {
    55	      return res
    56	        .status(409)
    57	        .json({ success: false, error: "Event time is outside available time slots" });
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    const participantEmails = emails ? emails.split(",").map((email) => email.trim()) : [];
    61	    const participants = await User.find({ email: { $in: participantEmails } });
    62	
    63	    if (participantEmails.length > 0 && participants.length !== participantEmails.length) {
    64	      const foundEmails = participants.map((user) => user.email);
    65	      const missingEmails = participantEmails.filter(
    66	        (email) => !foundEmails.includes(email)
    67	      );
    68	      return res.status(400).json({
    69	        success: false,
    70	        error: `These emails are not registered users: ${missingEmails.join(", ")}`,
    71	      });
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    // Create participant list
    75	    const participantList = participants.map((user) => ({
    76	      name: `${user.firstName} ${user.lastName}`,
    77	      user: user._id,
    78	      status: "pending",
    79	    }));
    80	
    81	    // Optionally add the creator as an accepted participant (uncomment if needed)
    82	    // participantList.push({
    83	    //   name: `${req.user.firstName} ${req.user.lastName}`,
    84	    //   user: req.user.id,
    85	    //   status: "accepted",
    86	    // });
    87	
    88	    // Step 4: Create and save the event
    89	    const event = new Event({
    90	      title,
    91	      description,
    92	      dateTime: eventStart,
    93	      duration,
    94	      link,
    95	      bannerText,
    96	      backgroundColor,
    97	      password: password ? await bcrypt.hash(password, 10) : undefined,
    98	      participants: participantList,
    99	      createdBy: req.user.id,
   100	    });
   101	
   102	    await event.save();
   103	    res.status(201).json({ success: true, message: "Event created successfully" });
   104	  } catch (error) {
   105	    console.error("Error creating event:", error);
   106	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: "Server error" });
   107	  }
   108	});
   109	
   110	//get events status wise
   111	router.get("/userMeetings", auth, async (req, res) => {
   112	  try {
   113	    const now = new Date();
   114	    const query = {
   115	      $or: [{ createdBy: req.user.id }, { "participants.user": req.user.id }],
   116	    };
   117	    const meetings = await Event.find(query)
   118	      .populate("createdBy", "name email")
   119	      .populate("participants.user", "name email");
   120	
   121	    const categorizedMeetings = {
   122	      upcoming: meetings.filter((m) => {
   123	        const isUpcoming = new Date(m.dateTime).getTime() > now.getTime(); // Check if the event is in the future
   124	        const isCreator = m.createdBy._id.toString() === req.user.id;
   125	        const participant = m.participants.find(
   126	          (p) => p.user && p.user._id.toString() === req.user.id
   127	        );
   128	        return isUpcoming && (isCreator || (participant && participant.status === "accepted"));
   129	      }),
   130	      past: meetings.filter((m) => {
   131	        const isPast = new Date(m.dateTime).getTime() + m.duration * 60000 < now.getTime();
   132	        const isCreator = m.createdBy._id.toString() === req.user.id;
   133	        const participant = m.participants.find(
   134	          (p) => p.user && p.user._id.toString() === req.user.id
   135	        );
   136	        return isPast && (isCreator || participant);
   137	      }),
   138	      pending: meetings.filter((m) =>{
   139	        const isCreator = m.createdBy._id.toString() === req.user.id;
   140	        const participant = m.participants.find(
   141	          (p) => p.user && p.user._id.toString() === req.user.id
   142	        );
   143	        return !isCreator && participant && participant.status === "pending";
   144	    }),
   145	      cancelled: meetings.filter((m) =>{
   146	        const isCreator = m.createdBy._id.toString() === req.user.id;
   147	        const participant = m.participants.find(
   148	          (p) => p.user && p.user._id.toString() === req.user.id
   149	        );
   150	        return !isCreator && participant && participant.status === "rejected";
   151	      }
   152	      ),
   153	    };
   154	    res.json({ success: true, events: categorizedMeetings });
   155	  } catch (error) {
   156	
   157	    console.log(error);
   158	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server error" });
   159	  }
   160	});
   161	
   162	// Get Events (with pagination)
   163	router.get("/", auth, async (req, res) => {
   164	  const { page = 1, limit = 10} = req.query;
   165	  try {
   166	    const query = {
   167	      $or: [{ createdBy: req.user.id }],
   168	    };
   169	    const events = await Event.find(query)
   170	      .populate("createdBy", "name email")
   171	      .populate("participants.user", "name email")
   172	      .skip((page - 1) * limit)
   173	      .limit(parseInt(limit))
   174	      .sort({ dateTime: 1 });
   175	    const total = await Event.countDocuments(query);
   176	    res.json({
   177	      success: true,
   178	      events,
   179	      total,
   180	      page: parseInt(page),
   181	      limit: parseInt(limit),
   182	    });
   183	  } catch (error) {
   184	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
   185	  }
   186	});
   187	
   188	// Update Event
   189	router.put("/:id", auth, async (req, res) => {
   190	  try {
   191	    const event = await Event.findOneAndUpdate(
   192	      { _id: req.params.id, createdBy: req.user.id },
   193	      { ...req.body, updatedAt: Date.now() },
   194	      { new: true }
   195	    );
   196	    if (!event)
   197	      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Event not found" });
   198	    res.json( { success: true, message: "Event updated successfully", event });
   199	  } catch (error) {
   200	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
   201	  }
   202	});
   203	// update participant status
   204	router.put("/status/:id", auth, async (req, res) => {
   205	  const { id } = req.params;
   206	  const { status } = req.body;
   207	
   208	  try {
   209	    const event = await Event.findById(id);
   210	    if (!event) return res.status(404).json({ message: "Meeting not found" });
   211	
   212	    const participant = event.participants.find(
   213	      (p) => p.user._id.toString() === req.user.id
   214	    );
   215	
   216	    if (!participant)
   217	      return res
   218	        .status(403)
   219	        .json({ success: false, message: "Not a participant" });
   220	
   221	    participant.status = status;
   222	    await event.save();
   223	
   224	    res.json({ success: true, message: "Status updated successfully" });
   225	  } catch (error) {
   226	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: "Server error" });
   227	  }
   228	});
   229	
   230	// Delete Event
   231	router.delete("/:id", auth, async (req, res) => {
   232	  try {
   233	    const event = await Event.findOneAndDelete({
   234	      _id: req.params.id,
   235	      createdBy: req.user.id,
   236	    });
   237	    if (!event) return res.status(404).json({ error: "Event not found" });
   238	    res.json({ success: true, message: "Event deleted" });
   239	  } catch (error) {
   240	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
   241	  }
   242	});
   243	
   244	// Join Event (Public Route)
   245	router.post("/join/:id", async (req, res) => {
   246	  const { password } = req.body;
   247	  try {
   248	    const event = await Event.findById(req.params.id);
   249	    if (!event)
   250	      return res.status(404).json({ success: false, error: "Event not found" });
   251	    if (event.password && !(await bcrypt.compare(password, event.password))) {
   252	      return res
   253	        .status(401)
   254	        .json({ success: false, error: "Invalid password" });
   255	    }
   256	    res.json({ event });
   257	  } catch (error) {
   258	    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: error.message });
   259	  }
   260	});
   261	
   262	module.exports = router;

=================

File: ./backend/server.js
----------------
     1	const express = require('express');
     2	const dotenv = require('dotenv');
     3	const cors = require('cors');
     4	const connectDB = require('./config/db');
     5	
     6	dotenv.config();
     7	const app = express();
     8	
     9	// Middleware
    10	app.use(express.json());
    11	app.use(cors());
    12	
    13	// Connect to MongoDB
    14	connectDB();
    15	
    16	// Routes
    17	app.use('/api/auth', require('./routes/auth'));
    18	app.use('/api/events', require('./routes/events'));
    19	app.use('/api/availability', require('./routes/availability'));
    20	
    21	app.get('/',(req,res)=>{
    22	    res.send('hello')
    23	})
    24	
    25	const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
    26	app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`Server running on port ${PORT}`));

File: ./frontend/README.md
----------------
     1	# React + Vite
     2	
     3	This template provides a minimal setup to get React working in Vite with HMR and some ESLint rules.
     4	
     5	Currently, two official plugins are available:
     6	
     7	- [@vitejs/plugin-react](https://github.com/vitejs/vite-plugin-react/blob/main/packages/plugin-react/README.md) uses [Babel](https://babeljs.io/) for Fast Refresh
     8	- [@vitejs/plugin-react-swc](https://github.com/vitejs/vite-plugin-react-swc) uses [SWC](https://swc.rs/) for Fast Refresh
     9	
    10	## Expanding the ESLint configuration
    11	
    12	If you are developing a production application, we recommend using TypeScript and enable type-aware lint rules. Check out the [TS template](https://github.com/vitejs/vite/tree/main/packages/create-vite/template-react-ts) to integrate TypeScript and [`typescript-eslint`](https://typescript-eslint.io) in your project.

File: ./frontend/src/components/auth/Login.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2	import styles from '../../styles/Auth.module.css';
     3	import authImg from '../../assets/auth_bg.png';
     4	import { Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
     5	import axios from 'axios';
     6	
     7	import Header from '../layout/Header';
     8	
     9	function Login() {
    10	const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    11	    firstName:"",
    12	    lastName:"",
    13	    email:"",
    14	    password:"",
    15	    confirmPassword:"",
    16	  })
    17	
    18	  const [error, setError] = useState('');
    19	
    20	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    21	
    22	  const handleChange = (e)=>{
    23	    const {name, value} = e.target;
    24	    setFormData((prev)=>({...prev, [name]:value}))
    25	  }
    26	
    27	  const handleSubmit = (e)=>{
    28	    e.preventDefault();
    29	    axios.post('`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/auth/login', formData)`
    30	    .then((response)=>{
    31	        if(response.data.success){
    32	          localStorage.setItem('token', response.data.token);
    33	          localStorage.setItem('user', JSON.stringify(response.data.user));
    34	          navigate('/dashboard')
    35	        }else{
    36	        }
    37	    })
    38	    .catch((err)=>{
    39	      console.log(err.response.data.error)
    40	      err.response ? setError(err.response.data.error):"An error occured"
    41	    })
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  return (
    45	    <div className={styles.container}>
    46	      <Header />
    47	      <div className={styles.formContainer}>
    48	          <div className={styles.formHeaderSignin}>
    49	              <h1>Sign in to your Spark</h1>
    50	          </div>
    51	          <form className={styles.form} onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
    52	            <label htmlFor ='firstName' className={styles.label} >First Name</label>
    53	            <input type="email" name='email' className={styles.input} value={formData.email} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    54	            <label htmlFor = 'password' className={styles.label} >Password</label>
    55	            <input type="password" name='password' className={styles.input} value={formData.password} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    56	            <button type="submit" className={styles.btn} >Login</button>
    57	            <p>Don't have an account? <Link to="/signup">Sign up</Link></p>
    58	            {
    59	            error && <p style={{color:'red'}}>{error}</p>
    60	          }
    61	          </form>
    62	          <p>This site is protected by reCAPTCHA and the Google Privacy Policy and Terms of Service apply.</p>
    63	      </div>
    64	      <div className={styles.imageContainer}>
    65	        <img src={authImg} alt="auth image bg" />
    66	      </div>
    67	
    68	    </div>
    69	  )}
    70	
    71	export default Login;

File: ./frontend/src/components/auth/Signup.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, {useState} from 'react'
     2	import axios from 'axios' 
     3	import {Link, useNavigate} from 'react-router-dom'
     4	
     5	import styles from '../../styles/Auth.module.css'
     6	import authImg from '../../assets/auth_bg.png'
     7	
     8	import Headers from '../layout/Header'
     9	
    10	function Signup() {
    11	
    12	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    13	    firstName:"",
    14	    lastName:"",
    15	    email:"",
    16	    password:"",
    17	    confirmPassword:"",
    18	  })
    19	
    20	  const [error, setError] = useState('')
    21	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    22	
    23	  const handleChange = (e)=>{
    24	    const {name, value} = e.target;
    25	    setFormData((prev)=>({...prev, [name]:value}) )
    26	  }
    27	
    28	  const handleSubmit = async (event) => {
    29	    event.preventDefault();
    30	  
    31	    try {
    32	      const response = await axios.post('`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/auth/signup', formData); `
    33	      if (response.data.success) {
    34	        navigate('/login');
    35	      } else {
    36	        setError(response.data.message);
    37	      }
    38	    } catch (err) {
    39	      console.log(err.response.data.message);
    40	      setError(err.response ? err.response.data.message : 'An error occurred');
    41	    }
    42	  };
    43	
    44	  return (
    45	    <div className={styles.container}>
    46	      <Headers/>
    47	      <div className={styles.formContainer}>
    48	          <div className={styles.formHeader}>
    49	              <h1>Create an account</h1>
    50	              <Link to="/login">Sign in instead</Link>
    51	          </div>
    52	          <form className={styles.form} onSubmit={handleSubmit} >
    53	            <label htmlFor ='firstName' className={styles.label}>First Name</label>
    54	            <input type="text" name='firstName' className={styles.input} value={formData.firstName} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    55	            <label htmlFor = 'lastName' className={styles.label}>Last Name</label>
    56	            <input type="text" name='lastName' className={styles.input} value={formData.lastName} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    57	            <label htmlFor = 'email' className={styles.label}>Email</label>
    58	            <input type="email" name='email' className={styles.input} value={formData.email} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    59	            <label htmlFor = 'password' className={styles.label}>Password</label>
    60	            <input type="password" name='password' className={styles.input} value={formData.password} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    61	            <label htmlFor = 'confirmPassword' className={styles.label}>Confirm Password</label>
    62	            <input type="password" name='confirmPassword' className={styles.input} 
    63	            value={formData.confirmPassword} onChange={handleChange} required/>
    64	            <div className={styles.terms}>
    65	                <input type="checkbox" id="terms" required/>
    66	                <label htmlFor="terms">By creating an account I agree to our <a href="#">Terms of use</a> and <a href="#">Privacy Policy</a></label>
    67	            </div>
    68	            <button  className={styles.btn}  type="submit">Create an account</button>
    69	            {
    70	              error && <p style={{color:'red'}}>{error}</p>
    71	            }
    72	          </form>
    73	          <p>This site is protected by reCAPTCHA and the Google Privacy Policy and Terms of Service apply.</p>
    74	      </div>
    75	      <div className={styles.imageContainer}>
    76	        <img src={authImg} alt="auth image bg" />
    77	      </div>
    78	    </div>
    79	  )
    80	}

    82	export default Signup

File: ./frontend/src/components/availabilityScheduler/AvailabilityForm.jsx
----------------
     1	import React from "react";
     2	import styles from "../../styles/AvailabilityScheduler.module.css";
     3	
     4	const generateTimeOptions = () => {
     5	  let times = [];
     6	  for (let h = 0; h < 24; h++) {
     7	    for (let m = 0; m < 60; m += 15) {
     8	      let hour = h.toString().padStart(2, "0");
     9	      let minute = m.toString().padStart(2, "0");
    10	      times.push(`${hour}:${minute}`);
    11	    }
    12	  }
    13	  return times;
    14	};
    15	
    16	const timeOptions = generateTimeOptions();
    17	
    18	function AvailabilityForm({
    19	  days,
    20	  handleDayToggle,
    21	  handleTimeChange,
    22	  addTimeSlot,
    23	  removeTimeSlot,
    24	}) {
    25	  return (
    26	    <div>
    27	      <h2 className={styles.sectionTitle}>Weekly hours</h2>
    28	
    29	      {Object.keys(days).map((day) => (
    30	        <div key={day} className={styles.dayRow}>
    31	          <input
    32	            type="checkbox"
    33	            checked={days[day].checked}
    34	            onChange={() => handleDayToggle(day)}
    35	          />
    36	          <span className={styles.dayLabel}>{day}</span>
    37	          {days[day].checked ? (
    38	            <div className={styles.timeInputs}>
    39	              {days[day].times.length === 0 ? (
    40	                <span className={styles.unavailableText}>Unavailable</span>
    41	              ) : (
    42	                days[day].times.map((time, index) => {
    43	                  return (
    44	                    <div key={index} className={styles.timeInputs}>
    45	                      <input
    46	                        type="text"
    47	                        value={time.start}
    48	                        onChange={(e) =>
    49	                          handleTimeChange(day, index, "start", e.target.value)
    50	                        }
    51	                        className={styles.timeInput}
    52	                        placeholder="HH:MM"
    53	                        list={`time-options-${day}-${index}-start`}
    54	                      />
    55	                      <datalist id={`time-options-${day}-${index}-start`}>
    56	                        {timeOptions.map((t, i) => (
    57	                          <option key={i} value={t} />
    58	                        ))}
    59	                      </datalist>
    60	
    61	                      <span>-</span>
    62	
    63	                      <input
    64	                        type="text"
    65	                        value={time.end}
    66	                        onChange={(e) =>
    67	                          handleTimeChange(day, index, "end", e.target.value)
    68	                        }
    69	                        className={styles.timeInput}
    70	                        placeholder="HH:MM"
    71	                        list={`time-options-${day}-${index}-end`}
    72	                      />
    73	                      <datalist id={`time-options-${day}-${index}-end`}>
    74	                        {timeOptions.map((t, i) => (
    75	                          <option key={i} value={t} />
    76	                        ))}
    77	                      </datalist>
    78	
    79	                      <button
    80	                        onClick={() => removeTimeSlot(day, index)}
    81	                        className={styles.removeButton}
    82	                      >
    83	                        ✕
    84	                      </button>
    85	                    </div>
    86	                  );
    87	                })
    88	              )}
    89	              <button onClick={() => addTimeSlot(day)} className={styles.addButton}>
    90	                +
    91	              </button>
    92	            </div>
    93	          ) : (
    94	            <span className={styles.unavailableText}>Unavailable</span>
    95	          )}
    96	        </div>
    97	      ))}
    98	    </div>
    99	  );
   100	}
   101	
   102	export default AvailabilityForm;

File: ./frontend/src/components/availabilityScheduler/AvailabilityScheduler.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from "react";
     2	import axios from "axios";
     3	import styles from "../../styles/AvailabilityScheduler.module.css";
     4	
     5	import Tabs from "./Tabs";
     6	import Dropdowns from "./Dropdowns";
     7	import AvailabilityForm from "./AvailabilityForm";
     8	import CalendarView from "./CalendarView";
     9	
    10	function AvailabilityScheduler() {
    11	  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("Availability");
    12	  const [days, setDays] = useState({});
    13	
    14	  const [activity, setActivity] = useState("Event type");
    15	  const [timeZone, setTimeZone] = useState("India Standard Time");
    16	  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    17	  const [saveTimeout, setSaveTimeout] = useState(null);
    18	
    19	  useEffect(() => {
    20	    const fetchAvailability = async () => {
    21	      try {
    22	        setLoading(true);
    23	        const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    24	        const config = { headers: { Authorization: `${token}` } };
    25	        const response = await axios.get(
    26	          "`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/availability",`
    27	          config
    28	        );
    29	        if (response.data.success) {
    30	          setDays(response.data.availability.days);
    31	          setTimeZone(response.data.availability.timeZone);
    32	        }
    33	      } catch (error) {
    34	        console.error("Failed to fetch availability:", error);
    35	      } finally {
    36	        setLoading(false);
    37	      }
    38	    };
    39	    fetchAvailability();
    40	  }, []);
    41	
    42	  const saveAvailability = useCallback((updatedDays) => {
    43	    clearTimeout(saveTimeout);
    44	    const newTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
    45	      try {
    46	        const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    47	        const config = { headers: { Authorization: `${token}` } };
    48	
    49	        const filteredDays = Object.keys(updatedDays).reduce((acc, day) => {
    50	          acc[day] = {
    51	            ...updatedDays[day],
    52	            times: updatedDays[day].times.filter(
    53	              (time) => time.start.trim() !== "" && time.end.trim() !== ""
    54	            ),
    55	          };
    56	          return acc;
    57	        }, {});
    58	
    59	        const payload = { days: filteredDays, timeZone };
    60	        await axios.put("`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/availability", payload, config);`
    61	      } catch (error) {
    62	        console.error("Failed to save availability:", error);
    63	      }
    64	    }, 2000);
    65	
    66	    setSaveTimeout(newTimeout);
    67	  }, [timeZone, saveTimeout]);
    68	
    69	  const handleDayToggle = (day) => {
    70	    setDays((prev) => {
    71	      const updatedDays = {
    72	        ...prev,
    73	        [day]: { ...prev[day], checked: !prev[day].checked },
    74	      };
    75	      saveAvailability(updatedDays);
    76	      return updatedDays;
    77	    });
    78	  };
    79	
    80	  const handleTimeChange = (day, index, field, value) => {
    81	    setDays((prev) => {
    82	      const updatedTimes = [...prev[day].times];
    83	      updatedTimes[index] = { ...updatedTimes[index], [field]: value };
    84	      const updatedDays = {
    85	        ...prev,
    86	        [day]: { ...prev[day], times: updatedTimes },
    87	      };
    88	      saveAvailability(updatedDays);
    89	      return updatedDays;
    90	    });
    91	  };
    92	
    93	  const addTimeSlot = (day) => {
    94	    setDays((prev) => {
    95	      const updatedDays = {
    96	        ...prev,
    97	        [day]: {
    98	          ...prev[day],
    99	          times: [...prev[day].times, { start: "", end: "" }],
   100	        },
   101	      };
   102	      saveAvailability(updatedDays);
   103	      return updatedDays;
   104	    });
   105	  };
   106	
   107	  const removeTimeSlot = (day, index) => {
   108	    setDays((prev) => {
   109	      const updatedDays = {
   110	        ...prev,
   111	        [day]: {
   112	          ...prev[day],
   113	          times: prev[day].times.filter((_, i) => i !== index),
   114	        },
   115	      };
   116	      saveAvailability(updatedDays);
   117	      return updatedDays;
   118	    });
   119	  };
   120	
   121	  if (loading) {
   122	    return <div className={styles.container}>Loading availability...</div>;
   123	  }
   124	
   125	  return (
   126	    <div className={styles.container}>
   127	      <div className={styles.main}>
   128	        <h1 className={styles.header}>  Availability</h1>
   129	        <p className={styles.subHeader}>Configure times when you are available for bookings</p>
   130	        <Tabs activeTab={activeTab} setActiveTab={setActiveTab} />
   131	        <div className={styles.card}>
   132	          <Dropdowns
   133	            activity={activity}
   134	            setActivity={setActivity}
   135	            timeZone={timeZone}
   136	            setTimeZone={(value) => {
   137	              setTimeZone(value);
   138	              saveAvailability();
   139	            }}
   140	          />
   141	          {activeTab === "Availability" ? (
   142	            <AvailabilityForm
   143	              days={days}
   144	              handleDayToggle={handleDayToggle}
   145	              handleTimeChange={handleTimeChange}
   146	              addTimeSlot={addTimeSlot}
   147	              removeTimeSlot={removeTimeSlot}
   148	            />
   149	          ) : (
   150	            <CalendarView days={days} events={[]} />
   151	          )}
   152	        </div>
   153	      </div>
   154	    </div>
   155	  );
   156	}
   157	
   158	export default AvailabilityScheduler;

File: ./frontend/src/components/availabilityScheduler/CalendarView.jsx
----------------
     1	import React from 'react';
     2	import styles from '../../styles/AvailabilityScheduler.module.css'
     3	
     4	const CalendarView = ({ days, events }) => {
     5	  const timeToRow = (time) => {
     6	    const [hours, minutes] = time.split(':').map(Number);
     7	    return (hours - 9) * 2 + (minutes / 30) + 2;
     8	  };
     9	
    10	  const timeToSpan = (start, end) => {
    11	    const startMinutes = parseInt(start.split(':')[0]) * 60 + parseInt(start.split(':')[1]);
    12	    const endMinutes = parseInt(end.split(':')[0]) * 60 + parseInt(end.split(':')[1]);
    13	    return (endMinutes - startMinutes) / 30;
    14	  };
    15	
    16	  const weekDays = ['Sun', 'Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat'];
    17	  const dates = ['23', '24', '25', '26', '27', '28', '1'];
    18	
    19	  return (
    20	    <div>
    21	      <div className={styles.calendarControls}>
    22	        <div className={styles.navButtons}>
    23	          <button className={styles.navButton}>{'<'}</button>
    24	          <button className={styles.navButton}>Today</button>
    25	          <button className={styles.navButton}>{'>'}</button>
    26	        </div>
    27	        <div className={styles.viewButtons}>
    28	          <button className={styles.viewButton}>Day</button>
    29	          <button className={`${styles.viewButton} ${styles.active}`}>Week</button>
    30	          <button className={styles.viewButton}>Month</button>
    31	          <button className={styles.viewButton}>Year</button>
    32	        </div>
    33	        <div>
    34	          <input type="text" placeholder="Search" className={styles.searchInput} />
    35	        </div>
    36	      </div>
    37	
    38	      <div className={styles.calendarGrid}>
    39	        <div className={styles.timeColumn}>
    40	          <div className={styles.timeHeader}></div>
    41	          {[...Array(8)].map((_, i) => (
    42	            <div key={i} className={styles.timeSlot}>
    43	              {i + 9} {i + 9 < 12 ? 'AM' : 'PM'}
    44	            </div>
    45	          ))}
    46	        </div>
    47	
    48	        {weekDays.map((day, index) => (
    49	          <div key={day} className={styles.dayColumn}>
    50	            <div className={styles.dayHeader}>
    51	              {day} {dates[index]}
    52	            </div>
    53	            <div className={styles.dayGrid}>
    54	              {days[day].checked &&
    55	                days[day].times.map((time, i) => (
    56	                  <div
    57	                    key={i}
    58	                    className={styles.availabilitySlot}
    59	                    style={{
    60	                      gridRowStart: timeToRow(time.start),
    61	                      gridRowEnd: `span ${timeToSpan(time.start, time.end)}`,
    62	                    }}
    63	                  ></div>
    64	                ))}
    65	
    66	              {events
    67	                .filter((event) => event.day === day)
    68	                .map((event, i) => (
    69	                  <div
    70	                    key={i}
    71	                    className={`${styles.eventSlot} ${
    72	                      event.title === 'Meeting 2' ? styles.meeting2 : styles.meeting
    73	                    }`}
    74	                    style={{
    75	                      gridRowStart: timeToRow(event.start),
    76	                      gridRowEnd: `span ${timeToSpan(event.start, event.end)}`,
    77	                    }}
    78	                  >
    79	                    {event.start} - {event.title}
    80	                  </div>
    81	                ))}
    82	            </div>
    83	          </div>
    84	        ))}
    85	        <div className={styles.timeZoneIndicator}>EST (GMT-5)</div>
    86	      </div>
    87	    </div>
    88	  );
    89	};
    90	
    91	export default CalendarView;

File: ./frontend/src/components/booking/BookingCard.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { act, useState } from "react";
     2	import axios from "axios";
     3	import styles from "../../styles/BookingCard.module.css";
     4	
     5	import ParticipantDropdown from "./ParticipantDropdown";
     6	
     7	function BookingCard({ event, activeTab, refetchEvents }) {
     8	  const [showParticipants, setShowParticipants] = useState(false);
     9	  const [localStatus, setLocalStatus] = useState(activeTab);
    10	
    11	  const userId = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user")).id;
    12	  const handleEventAction = async (action) => {
    13	    const newStatus = action === "accept" ? "accepted" : "rejected";
    14	    try {
    15	      setLocalStatus(newStatus);
    16	      setShowParticipants(false);
    17	
    18	      const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    19	      const config = {
    20	        headers: {
    21	          Authorization: `${token}`,
    22	        },
    23	      };
    24	      await axios.put(
    25	        ``${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events/status/${event.id}`,`
    26	        { status: action === "accept" ? "accepted" : "rejected" },
    27	        config
    28	      );
    29	      // refetch the events
    30	      await refetchEvents();
    31	      setShowParticipants(false);
    32	    } catch (err) {
    33	      console.error("Failed to update event status:", err);
    34	      setLocalStatus(activeTab);
    35	    }
    36	  };
    37	
    38	  //setting status, if user is creator, get accepted
    39	  const displayStatus =
    40	    event.participantList.find((p) => {
    41	      return (p.userId === userId)
    42	    })?.status ||
    43	    "accepted";
    44	
    45	  return (
    46	    <div className={styles.eventCard}>
    47	      <div className={styles.eventDetails}>
    48	        <div className={styles.eventDateTime}>
    49	          <p>{event.date}</p>
    50	          <p>{event.time}</p>
    51	        </div>
    52	        <div className={styles.eventInfo}>
    53	          <p className={styles.eventTitle}>{event.title}</p>
    54	          <p>{"You and " + event.participantCount + " others"}</p>
    55	        </div>
    56	      </div>
    57	
    58	      <div className={styles.eventActions}>
    59	        {activeTab === "pending" ? (
    60	          <>
    61	            {/* <button className={styles.participantButton} onClick={() => setShowParticipants(!showParticipants)}>
    62	                Participant ({event.participantList?.length || 0})
    63	            </button> */}
    64	            {showParticipants && (
    65	              <ParticipantDropdown
    66	                participants={event.participantList || []}
    67	                onAccept={() => handleEventAction("accept")}
    68	                onReject={() => handleEventAction("reject")}
    69	              />
    70	            )}
    71	          </>
    72	        ) : activeTab === "past" ? (
    73	          displayStatus === "pending" ? (
    74	            <>
    75	              {showParticipants && (
    76	                <ParticipantDropdown
    77	                  participants={event.participantList || []}
    78	                  onAccept={() => handleEventAction("accept")}
    79	                  onReject={() => handleEventAction("reject")}
    80	                />
    81	              )}
    82	            </>
    83	          ) : (
    84	            <>
    85	              <button
    86	                className={`${styles.statusButton} ${
    87	                  displayStatus === "accepted"
    88	                    ? styles.accepted
    89	                    : styles.rejected
    90	                }`}
    91	              >
    92	                {displayStatus === "accepted" ? "Accepted" : "Rejected"}
    93	              </button>
    94	            </>
    95	          )
    96	        ) : (
    97	          <>
    98	            <button
    99	              className={`${styles.statusButton} ${
   100	                activeTab === "upcoming" ? styles.accepted : styles.rejected
   101	              }`}
   102	            >
   103	              {activeTab === "upcoming" ? "Accepted" : "Rejected"}
   104	            </button>
   105	          </>
   106	        )}
   107	        {event.participantCount && activeTab !== "cancelled" && (
   108	          <div
   109	            className={styles.participantCount}
   110	            onMouseOver={() => setShowParticipants(!showParticipants)}
   111	          >
   112	            <span role="img" aria-label="people">
   113	              👥
   114	            </span>{" "}
   115	            {event.participantCount} people
   116	          </div>
   117	        )}
   118	      </div>
   119	    </div>
   120	  );
   121	}
   122	export default BookingCard;

File: ./frontend/src/components/booking/Booking.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, {useState, useEffect} from 'react'
     2	import styles from '../../styles/Booking.module.css'
     3	import axios from 'axios'
     4	
     5	import BookingTabs from './BookingTabs';
     6	import BookingList from './BookingList';
     7	
     8	function Booking() {
     9	      const [events, setEvents] = useState({}
    10	        );
    11	
    12	    const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('upcoming');
    13	    const [error, setError] = useState('')
    14	    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
    15	    const [filteredEvents, setFilteredEvents] = useState([])
    16	        
    17	    //Transform the event array as per UI format
    18	    const transformEvents = (eventArray) => {
    19	      return eventArray.map((event) => ({
    20	        id: event._id,
    21	        date: new Date(event.dateTime).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    22	          weekday: 'long',
    23	          day: 'numeric',
    24	          month: 'short',
    25	        }),
    26	        time: `${new Date(event.dateTime).toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
    27	          hour: 'numeric',
    28	          minute: 'numeric',
    29	        })} - ${new Date(
    30	          new Date(event.dateTime).getTime() + event.duration * 60000
    31	        ).toLocaleTimeString('en-US', { hour: 'numeric', minute: 'numeric' })}`,
    32	        title: event.title,
    33	        participants: event.participants,
    34	        status: event.status,
    35	        participantCount: event.participants.length,
    36	        participantList: event.participants.map((p) => ({
    37	          name: p.name,
    38	          status: p.status,
    39	          userId: p.user._id,
    40	        })),
    41	      }));
    42	    };
    43	
    44	    const fetchEvents = async () => {
    45	      try {
    46	        setLoading(true);
    47	        const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    48	        if (!token) throw new Error('No authentication token found');
    49	  
    50	        const config = {
    51	          headers: {
    52	            Authorization: `${token}`,
    53	          },
    54	        };
    55	        const response = await axios.get('`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events/userMeetings', config);`
    56	        const fetchedEvents = response.data.events || {};
    57	        setEvents(fetchedEvents);
    58	  
    59	        // Set filteredEvents for the current active tab
    60	        const tabEvents = fetchedEvents[activeTab] || [];
    61	        const transformed = transformEvents(tabEvents);
    62	        setFilteredEvents(transformed);
    63	      } catch (err) {
    64	        setError(err.message || 'Failed to fetch events. Please try again later.');
    65	      } finally {
    66	        setLoading(false);
    67	      }
    68	    };
    69	  
    70	    useEffect(() => {
    71	      fetchEvents();
    72	    }, []);
    73	    const handleTabChange = (tab) => {
    74	      const tabEvents = events[tab] || [];
    75	      const transformed = transformEvents(tabEvents);
    76	      setFilteredEvents(transformed);
    77	      setActiveTab(tab);
    78	    };
    79	
    80	  return (
    81	    <div className={styles.cotainer}>
    82	        <div className={styles.bookingHead}>
    83	            <h1 className={styles.heading}>Booking</h1>
    84	            <p>See upcoming and past events booked through your event type links.</p>
    85	        </div>
    86	        <div className={styles.booking}>
    87	            <BookingTabs activeTab={activeTab} onTabChange={handleTabChange} />
    88	            {loading ? (
    89	              <div className={styles.loading}>Loading...</div>
    90	            ) : error ? (
    91	              <div className={styles.error}>{error}</div>
    92	            ) : (
    93	              <BookingList events={filteredEvents} activeTab={activeTab} refetchEvents={fetchEvents} />
    94	            )
    95	
    96	            }
    97	
    98	        </div>
    99	    </div>
   100	  )
   101	}
   102	
   103	export default Booking

File: ./frontend/src/components/booking/BookingTabs.jsx

     1	import React from 'react'
     2	import styles from '../../styles/BookingTabs.module.css'
     3	
     4	function BookingTabs({ activeTab, onTabChange }) {
     5	  const tabs = ['upcoming', 'pending', 'cancelled', 'past'];
     6	
     7	  return (
     8	    <div className={styles.tabs}>
     9	      {
    10	        tabs.map((tab, index) => (
    11	          <button
    12	          key={index}
    13	          className={`${styles.tab} ${activeTab === tab ? styles.active : ''}`}
    14	          onClick={() => onTabChange(tab)}
    15	        > 
    16	        {tab.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+tab.slice(1)} 
    17	        </button>
    18	        ))
    19	      }
    20	    </div>
    21	  )
    22	}

File: ./frontend/src/components/booking/ParticipantDropdown.jsx
----------------
     1	import React from "react";
     2	import PropTypes from "prop-types";
     3	import styles from "../../styles/ParticipantDropdown.module.css";
     4	
     5	import avatar from "../../assets/icons/avatar.png";
     6	import ApprovalButtons from "../ui/ApprovalButtons";
     7	
     8	const ParticipantDropdown = ({ participants, onAccept, onReject }) => {
     9	  return (
    10	    <div className={styles.participantDropdown}>
    11	      <div className={styles.participantHeader}>
    12	        <div className= {styles.participantTitle}><p>Participants</p> <span className={styles.participantCount}> ({participants.length})</span></div>
    13	        <ApprovalButtons onAccept={onAccept} onReject={onReject} />
    14	      </div>
    15	      <div className={styles.participantList}>
    16	        {participants.map((participant, index) => (
    17	          <div key={index} className={styles.participantItem}>
    18	            <img
    19	              src={avatar}
    20	              alt="Participant Avatar"
    21	              className={styles.participantAvatar}
    22	            />
    23	            <span>{participant.name}</span>
    24	            <input
    25	              type="checkbox"
    26	              checked={participant.status === "accepted"}
    27	              readOnly
    28	              disabled
    29	              className={styles.participantCheckbox}
    30	            />
    31	          </div>
    32	        ))}
    33	      </div>
    34	    </div>
    35	  );                
    36	};
    37	
    38	ParticipantDropdown.propTypes = {
    39	  participants: PropTypes.arrayOf(
    40	    PropTypes.shape({
    41	      name: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    42	      accepted: PropTypes.bool.isRequired,
    43	    })
    44	  ).isRequired,
    45	  onAccept: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
    46	  onReject: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
    47	};
    48	
    49	export default ParticipantDropdown;

File: ./frontend/src/components/Events/EventCard.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState } from "react";
     2	import axios from "axios";
     3	import styles from "../../styles/EventCard.module.css";
     4	import { showToast } from "../ui/ToastContainer";
     5	
     6	import copyBtn from "../../assets/icons/copyBtn.svg";
     7	import deleteBtn from "../../assets/icons/deleteBtn.svg";
     8	import editBtn from "../../assets/icons/editBtn.svg";
     9	import conflictIcon from "../../assets/icons/conflictIcon.svg";
    10	
    11	import Slider from "../ui/Slider";
    12	
    13	function EventCard({ title, date, startTime, endTime, description, 
    14	  status, id, eventLink, hasConflict, refetchEvents , event, onEdit}) {
    15	  const [active, setActive] = useState(status);
    16	  const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    17	
    18	  const handleSliderChange = async () => {
    19	    try {
    20	      const newStatus = active === "active" ? "deactivated" : "active";
    21	      await axios.put(``${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events/${id}`, { status: newStatus }, {`
    22	        headers: { Authorization: `${token}` }
    23	      });
    24	      setActive(newStatus);
    25	      showToast()(`Event ${newStatus}`);
    26	    } catch (error) {
    27	      console.error("Error updating event status:", error);
    28	    }
    29	  };
    30	
    31	  const handleCopyEvent = async () => {
    32	    try {
    33	      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(eventLink);
    34	      showToast()("Event link copied to clipboard!");
    35	    } catch (error) {
    36	      showToast()(error.message, "error");
    37	      console.error("Error copying event link:", error);
    38	    }
    39	  };
    40	
    41	  const handleDeleteEvent = async () => {
    42	    try {
    43	      await axios.delete(``${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events/${id}`, {`
    44	        headers: { Authorization: `${token}` }
    45	      });
    46	      showToast()("Event deleted successfully!");
    47	      refetchEvents();
    48	    } catch (error) {
    49	      showToast()(error.message, "error");
    50	      console.error("Error deleting event:", error);
    51	    }
    52	  };
    53	  
    54	  return (
    55	    <div className={styles.card}>
    56	      <div className={`${styles.line } ${styles[active]}`}></div>
    57	      {hasConflict && <div className={styles.conflictContainer}>
    58	        <img src={conflictIcon} alt="" className={styles.conflictIcon} /> 
    59	        <span className={styles.conflict}>Conflict of timing</span>
    60	        </div>}
    61	      <div className={styles.content}>
    62	        <div className={styles.cardHeader}>
    63	          <p className={styles.title}>{title}</p>
    64	          <img src={editBtn} alt="" onClick={() => onEdit(event)} className={styles.action} />
    65	        </div>
    66	        <p className={styles.cardDetails}>
    67	        <span className={styles.date}>{date}</span>
    68	        <br />
    69	        <span className={styles.time}>{startTime} - {endTime}</span>
    70	        <br />
    71	        <span className={styles.description}>{description}</span>
    72	      </p>
    73	      </div>
    74	      <hr className={styles.divider} />
    75	      <div className={styles.cardFooter}>
    76	        <Slider  checked={active==="active"} onChange={handleSliderChange} />
    77	        {/* <span className={styles.icon} onClick={handleCopyEvent}>📋</span> */}
    78	        <img src={copyBtn} alt="" className={styles.action} onClick={handleCopyEvent} />
    79	        <img src={deleteBtn} alt="" className={styles.action} onClick={handleDeleteEvent} />
    80	      </div>
    81	    </div>
    82	  );
    83	}
    84	
    85	export default EventCard;

    10	  const [step, setStep] = useState(1);
    11	  const [isBannerEditable, setIsBannerEditable] = useState(false);
    12	
    13	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState(initialData || {
    14	    title: "Event",
    15	    password: "123456",
    16	    hostName: "Sarthak Pal",
    17	    description: "Test Event",
    18	    date: "12/12/25",
    19	    time: "02:30",
    20	    period: "PM",
    21	    timezone: "UTC+5:00 (Delhi)",
    22	    duration: "1 hour",
    23	    backgroundColor: "#000000",
    24	    link: "https://zoom.us",

    26	    bannerText: "Test Event",
    27	  });
    28	
    29	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    30	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    31	    setFormData((prev) => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
    32	  };
    33	
    34	  const parseDDMMYY = (dateStr, time, period) => {
    35	    const [day, month, year] = dateStr.split('/').map(Number);
    36	    let hours = parseInt(time.split(':')[0], 10);
    37	    const minutes = parseInt(time.split(':')[1], 10);
    38	
    39	    if (period === 'PM' && hours !== 12) hours += 12;
    40	    if (period === 'AM' && hours === 12) hours = 0;
    41	
    42	    const fullYear = year < 100 ? 2000 + year : year;
    43	    const date = new Date(fullYear, month - 1, day, hours, minutes);
    44	
    45	    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) {
    46	      return null;
    47	    }
    48	    return date;
    49	  };
    50	
    51	  const handleNextStep = (event) => {
    52	    event.preventDefault();
    53	
    54	    // Validate Step 1 fields before proceeding
    55	    const { date, time, period } = formData;
    56	    const dateTime = parseDDMMYY(date, time, period);
    57	    if (!dateTime) {
    58	      showToast('Invalid date format. Please use DD/MM/YY (e.g., 12/12/25).', 'error');
    59	      return;
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    if (!formData.title || !formData.hostName) {
    63	      showToast('Please fill all required fields.', 'error');
    64	      return;
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    setStep(2); // Move to the second frame
    68	  };
    69	
    70	  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    71	    event.preventDefault();
    72	
    73	    const { date, time, period, duration, ...rest } = formData;
    74	    const dateTime = parseDDMMYY(date, time, period);
    75	    if (!dateTime) {
    76	      showToast('Invalid date format. Please use DD/MM/YY (e.g., 12/12/25).', 'error');
    77	      return;
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    const durationInMinutes = parseInt(duration.split(' ')[0]) * (duration.includes('hour') ? 60 : 1);
    81	
    82	    const payload = {
    83	      ...rest,
    84	      dateTime: dateTime.toISOString(),
    85	      duration: durationInMinutes,
    86	    };
    87	
    88	    const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    89	    if (!token) {
    90	      showToast('No token found. Please log in.', 'error');
    91	      return;
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    const config = {
    95	      headers: {
    96	        Authorization: `${token}`,
    97	      },
    98	    };
    99	
   100	    axios
   101	      .post("`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events", payload, config)`
   102	      .then((response) => {
   103	        if (response.data.success) {
   104	          showToast()("Successfully added event", "success");
   105	          refetchEvents();
   106	          onClose();
   107	        } else {
   108	          showToast()(response.data.error, "error");
   109	        }
   110	      })
   111	      .catch((err) => {
   112	        const errorMessage = err.response?.data?.error || 'An error occurred';
   113	        showToast()(errorMessage, "error");
   114	        console.error(err);
   115	      });
   116	  };
   117

   131

   133	          <form onSubmit={handleNextStep} className={styles.form}>
   134	            {/* Event Topic */}
   135	            <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   136	              <label className={styles.label}>
   137	                Event Topic <span className={styles.required}>*</span>
   138	              </label>
   139	              <input
   140	                type="text"
   141	                name="title"
   142	                value={formData.title}
   143	                onChange={handleChange}
   144	                placeholder="Set a conference topic before it starts"
   145	                className={styles.input}
   146	                required
   147	              />
   148	            </div>
   149	
   150	            {/* Password */}
   151	            <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   152	              <label className={styles.label}>Password</label>
   153	              <input
   154	                type="password"
   155	                name="password"
   156	                value={formData.password}
   157	                onChange={handleChange}

   159	                className={styles.input}

   166	                Host name <span className={styles.required}>*</span>
   167	              </label>
   168	              <select
   169	                name="hostName"
   170	                value={formData.hostName}
   171	                onChange={handleChange}
   172	                className={styles.select}
   173	                required
   174	              >
   175	                <option value="Sarthak Pal">Sarthak Pal</option>
   176	              </select>
   177	            </div>
   178	
   179	            {/* Description */}
   180	            <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   181	              <label className={styles.label}>Description</label>
   182	              <textarea
   183	                name="description"
   184	                value={formData.description}
   185	                onChange={handleChange}
   186	                className={styles.textarea}
   187	              />
   188	            </div>
   189	
   190	            <hr className={styles.modalHr} />
   191	
   192	            {/* Date and Time */}

   196	              </label>

   198	                <input

   203	                  placeholder="DD/MM/YY"

   205	                  required

File: ./frontend/src/components/Events/EventList.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
     2	import EventForm from './EventForm';
     3	import styles from "../../styles/EventList.module.css";
     4	import EventCard from "./EventCard";
     5	import axios from "axios";
     6	
     7	import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
     8	
     9	function EventList() {
    10	  const [events, setEvents] = useState([]);
    11	
    12	  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false);
    13	
    14	  const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    15	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    16	
    17	const fetchData = async () => {
    18	    try {
    19	      const response = await axios.get('`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/events/', {`
    20	        headers: {
    21	          Authorization: `${token}`,
    22	        },
    23	      });
    24	      if (!response.data.success) {
    25	        navigate('/login');
    26	        return;
    27	      }
    28	      const fetchedEvents = response.data.events;
    29	      // Add conflict detection
    30	      const eventsWithConflicts = fetchedEvents.map((event, index) => {
    31	        let hasConflict = false;
    32	      
    33	        const eventDateTime = new Date(event.dateTime);
    34	        const eventEndTime = new Date(
    35	          eventDateTime.getTime() + parseInt(event.duration) * 60 * 1000
    36	        );
    37	      
    38	        for (let i = 0; i < fetchedEvents.length; i++) {
    39	          if (i === index) continue;
    40	          const otherEvent = fetchedEvents[i];
    41	          const otherDateTime = new Date(otherEvent.dateTime);
    42	          const otherEndTime = new Date(
    43	            otherDateTime.getTime() + parseInt(otherEvent.duration) * 60 * 1000
    44	          );
    45	      
    46	          if (
    47	            eventDateTime.toDateString() === otherDateTime.toDateString() && // Ensure same date
    48	            ((eventDateTime >= otherDateTime && eventDateTime < otherEndTime) ||
    49	            (eventEndTime > otherDateTime && eventEndTime <= otherEndTime))
    50	          ) {
    51	            hasConflict = true;
    52	            break;
    53	          }
    54	        }
    55	        
    56	        return { ...event, hasConflict };
    57	      });
    58	      
    59	      setEvents(eventsWithConflicts);
    60	      
    61	    } catch (error) {
    62	      console.log(error);
    63	      navigate('/login');
    64	    }
    65	  };
    66	
    67	  useEffect(() => {
    68	    fetchData();
    69	  }, []);
    70	
    71	  const handleAddEvent = () => {
    72	    setIsModalOpen(true);
    73	  };
    74	
    75	  const handleCloseModal = () => {
    76	    setIsModalOpen(false);
    77	  };
    78	  function minutesToFormattedHours(minutes) {
    79	    const hours = minutes / 60; 
    80	    const wholeHours = Math.floor(hours); 
    81	    const decimalHours = (hours - wholeHours).toFixed(1); 
    82	    if (wholeHours > 0) {
    83	        return wholeHours + (decimalHours > 0 ? decimalHours : ''); 
    84	    } else {
    85	        return decimalHours;
    86	    }
    87	}
    88	
    89	const [selectedEvent, setSelectedEvent] = useState(null);
    90	
    91	const handleEditEvent = (event) => {
    92	  setSelectedEvent(event);
    93	  setIsModalOpen(true);
    94	};
    95	
    96	if(isModalOpen) return <EventForm onClose={handleCloseModal} refetchEvents={fetchData} initialData={selectedEvent}/>
    97	
    98	  return (
    99	    <div className={styles.container}>
   100	      <div className={styles.header}>
   101	        <div>
   102	          <h1 className={styles.headerTitle}>Event Types</h1>
   103	          <p className={styles.headerSubtitle}>
   104	            Create events to share for people to book on your calendar.
   105	          </p>
   106	        </div>
   107	        <button className={styles.addButton} onClick={handleAddEvent} >
   108	          <span className={styles.addIcon}>+</span> Add New Event
   109	        </button>
   110	      </div>
   111	      <div className={styles.eventList}>
   112	        {events.length > 0 ? (
   113	          events.map((event, index) => {
   114	            const startTime = new Date(event.dateTime);
   115	          const endTime = new Date(
   116	            startTime.getTime() + parseInt(event.duration) *60*1000
   117	          );
   118	            return (
   119	            <EventCard
   120	              key={event._id || index}
   121	              title={event.title}
   122	              date={startTime.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
   123	                weekday: 'long',
   124	                day: 'numeric',
   125	                month: 'short',
   126	              })}
   127	              startTime={startTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
   128	                hour: 'numeric',
   129	                minute: 'numeric',
   130	              })}
   131	              endTime={endTime.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
   132	                hour: 'numeric',
   133	                minute: 'numeric',
   134	              })}
   135	              description={`${minutesToFormattedHours(event.duration)}hr, ${event.description.slice(0, 50)}`}
   136	              status={event.status}
   137	              id={event._id}
   138	              eventLink = {event.link}
   139	              hasConflict={event.hasConflict}
   140	              refetchEvents={fetchData}
   141	              setIsModalOpen={setIsModalOpen}
   142	              event={event}
   143	              onEdit={handleEditEvent}
   144	            />
   145	          )})
   146	        ) : (
   147	          <div>No events found</div>
   148	        )}
   149	      </div>
   150	    </div>
   151	  );
   152	}
   153	
   154	export default EventList;

File: ./frontend/src/components/layout/UserProfile.jsx

     1	import React, { useState } from "react";
     2	import styles from "../../styles/UserProfile.module.css";
     3	import avatar from "../../assets/icons/avatar.png";
     4	import logoutIcon from "../../assets/icons/logoutIcon.svg";
     5	import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
     6	
     7	const UserProfile = () => {
     8	  const [logout, setLogout] = useState(false);
     9	  const userName = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user")).name;
    10	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    11	
    12	  const handleLogout = () => {
    13	    localStorage.removeItem("token");
    14	    localStorage.removeItem("name");
    15	    navigate("/login");
    16	  };
    17	  const handleMouseClick = () => {
    18	    setLogout(!logout);
    19	  };
    20	
    21	  return (
    22	    <div className={styles.container}>
    23	      {logout && (
    24	        <div className={styles.logout} onClick={handleLogout}>
    25	          <img
    26	            src={logoutIcon}
    27	            alt="User Avatar"
    28	            className={styles.logoutIcon}
    29	          />
    30	          <p>Sign out</p>
    31	        </div>
    32	      )}
    33	      <div className={styles.userProfile} onClick={handleMouseClick}>
    34	        <img src={avatar} alt="User Avatar" className={styles.userAvatar} />
    35	        <span className={styles.userName}>{userName}</span>
    36	      </div>
    37	    </div>
    38	  );
    39	};
    40	
    41	export default UserProfile;
