File: ./frontend/src/components/settings/ProfileForm.jsx
----------------
     1	import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";
     2	import styles from "../../styles/ProfileForm.module.css";
     3	import axios from "axios";
     4	import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
     5	
     6	import { showToast } from "../ui/ToastContainer";
     7	
     8	function ProfileForm() {
     9	  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    10	    firstName: "",
    11	    lastName: "",
    12	    email: "",
    13	    password: "",
    14	    confirmPassword: "",
    15	  });
    16	  const navigate = useNavigate();
    17	
    18	  useEffect(() => {
    19	    const fetchUserData = async () => {
    20	      try {
    21	        const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    22	        const response = await axios.get(
    23	          "`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/auth/profile",`
    24	          {
    25	            headers: {
    26	              Authorization: `${token}`,
    27	            },
    28	          }
    29	        );
    30	        const { firstName, lastName, email } = response.data.user;
    31	        setFormData({
    32	          firstName: firstName || "",
    33	          lastName: lastName || "",
    34	          email: email || "", 
    35	          password: "",
    36	          confirmPassword: "",
    37	        });
    38	      } catch (error) {
    39	        console.error("Error fetching user data:", error);
    40	      }
    41	    };
    42	
    43	    fetchUserData();
    44	  }, []);
    45	
    46	  const handleChange = (e) => {
    47	    const { name, value } = e.target;
    48	    setFormData((prev) => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
    49	  };
    50	  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    51	    e.preventDefault();
    52	    const token = localStorage.getItem("token");
    53	    const config = {
    54	      headers: {
    55	        Authorization: `${token}`,
    56	      },
    57	    };
    58	
    59	    axios
    60	      .put("`${import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL}/api/auth/profile", formData, config)`
    61	      .then((response) => {
    62	        if (response.data.shouldLogout) {
    63	          localStorage.removeItem("token");
    64	          navigate("/login");
    65	        } else {
    66	          navigate("/dashboard");
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        showToast()(response.data.message, "success")
    70	      })
    71	      .catch((err) => {
    72	        console.log(err.response.data.error);
    73	      });
    74	  };
    75	
    76	  return (
    77	    <div className={styles.container}>
    78	      <div className={styles.header}>
    79	        <div>
    80	          <h1 className={styles.headerTitle}>Profile</h1>
    81	          <p className={styles.headerSubtitle}>
    82	            Manage settings for your profile
    83	          </p>
    84	        </div>
    85	      </div>
    86	      <div className={styles.formContainer}>
    87	        <div className={styles.formHeader}>
    88	          <p className={`${styles.formTitle} ${styles.active}`}>Edit Profile</p>
    89	        </div>
    90	        <form className={styles.form} onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
    91	          <div className={styles.formGroup}>
    92	            <label htmlFor="firstName">First Name</label>
    93	            <input
    94	              type="text"
    95	              name="firstName"
    96	              value={formData.firstName}
    97	              onChange={handleChange}
    98	              required
    99	            />
   100	          </div>
   101	          <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   102	            <label htmlFor="lastName">Last Name</label>
   103	            <input
   104	              type="text"
   105	              name="lastName"
   106	              value={formData.lastName}
   107	              onChange={handleChange}
   108	              required
   109	            />
   110	          </div>
   111	          <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   112	            <label htmlFor="email">Email</label>
   113	            <input
   114	              type="email"
   115	              name="email"
   116	              value={formData.email}
   117	              onChange={handleChange}
   118	              required
   119	            />
   120	          </div>
   121	          <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   122	            <label htmlFor="password">Password</label>
   123	            <input
   124	              type="password"
   125	              name="password"
   126	              value={formData.password}
   127	              onChange={handleChange}
   128	            />
   129	          </div>
   130	          <div className={styles.formGroup}>
   131	            <label htmlFor="confirmPassword">Confirm Password</label>
   132	            <input
   133	              type="password"
   134	              name="confirmPassword"
   135	              value={formData.confirmPassword}
   136	              onChange={handleChange}
   137	            />
   138	          </div>
   139	          <button className={styles.submitBtn} type="submit">Save</button>
   140	        </form>
   141	      </div>
   142	    </div>
   143	  );
   144	}
   145	
   146	export default ProfileForm;

     1	import React, { useState } from 'react';
     2	import styles from '../../styles/Test.module.css'; // Assuming you have a CSS module for styling
     3	
     4	const Test = () => {
     5	  // State to manage the active tab
     6	  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('upcoming');
     7	
     8	  // State to manage event statuses (for accept/reject functionality in Pending tab)
     9	  const [events, setEvents] = useState([
    10	    {
    11	      id: 1,
    12	      date: 'Friday, 28 Feb',
    13	      time: '2:35 PM - 3:00 PM',
    14	      title: 'Appointment',

    24	      participantCount: 13,
    25	      status: 'upcoming',
    26	    },
    27	    {
    28	      id: 3,
    29	      date: 'Friday, 28 Feb',
    30	      time: '10:30 AM - 12:30 PM',
    31	      title: 'Meeting',
    32	      participants: ['You', 'Team 1'],
    33	      participantCount: 4,
    34	      status: 'pending',
    35	      participantList: [
    36	        { name: 'Akbar Husain', accepted: true },
    37	        { name: 'Aneesh Menon', accepted: false },
    38	        { name: 'Rahul Saini', accepted: false },
    39	        { name: 'Bharat Thakur', accepted: false },
    40	        { name: 'Natalia', accepted: false },
    41	        { name: 'Alia Toy', accepted: false },
    42	      ],
    43	    },
    44	  ]);
    45	
    46	  // State to manage the visibility of the participant dropdown
    47	  const [showParticipants, setShowParticipants] = useState(null);
    48	
    49	  // Function to handle tab switching
    50	  const handleTabChange = (tab) => {
    51	    setActiveTab(tab);
    52	    setShowParticipants(null); // Close participant dropdown when switching tabs
    53	  };
    54	
    55	  // Function to handle accept/reject for pending events
    56	  const handleEventAction = (eventId, action) => {
    57	    setEvents((prevEvents) =>
    58	      prevEvents.map((event) => {
    59	        if (event.id === eventId) {
    60	          return {
    61	            ...event,
    62	            status: action === 'accept' ? 'upcoming' : 'cancelled',
    63	          };
    64	        }
    65	        return event;
    66	      })
    67	    );
    68	    setShowParticipants(null); // Close participant dropdown after action
    69	  };
    70	
    71	  // Filter events based on the active tab
    72	  const filteredEvents = events.filter((event) => event.status === activeTab);
    73	
    74	  return (
    75	    <div className={styles.container}>
    76	      {/* Sidebar */}
    77	      <div className={styles.sidebar}>
    78	        <div className={styles.logo}>CNNCT</div>
    79	        <div className={styles.menu}>
    80	          <div className={styles.menuItem}>Events</div>
    81	          <div className={styles.menuItemActive}>Booking</div>
    82	          <div className={styles.menuItem}>Availability</div>
    83	          <div className={styles.menuItem}>Settings</div>
    84	        </div>
    85	        <div className={styles.user}>
    86	          <img src="https://via.placeholder.com/40" alt="User Avatar" className={styles.avatar} />
    87	          <span>Sarthak Pal</span>
    88	        </div>
    89	      </div>
    90	
    91	      {/* Main Content */}
    92	      <div className={styles.mainContent}>
    93	        <h1>Booking</h1>
    94	        <p className={styles.subtitle}>
    95	          See upcoming and past events booked through your event type links.
    96	        </p>
    97	
    98	        {/* Tabs */}
    99	        <div className={styles.tabs}>
   100	          <button
   101	            className={`${styles.tab} ${activeTab === 'upcoming' ? styles.active : ''}`}
   102	            onClick={() => handleTabChange('upcoming')}
   103	          >
   104	            Upcoming
   105	          </button>
   106	          <button
   107	            className={`${styles.tab} ${activeTab === 'pending' ? styles.active : ''}`}
   108	            onClick={() => handleTabChange('pending')}
   109	          >
   110	            Pending
   111	          </button>
   112	          <button
   113	            className={`${styles.tab} ${activeTab === 'cancelled' ? styles.active : ''}`}
   114	            onClick={() => handleTabChange('cancelled')}
   115	          >
   116	            Cancelled
   117	          </button>
   118	          <button
   119	            className={`${styles.tab} ${activeTab === 'past' ? styles.active : ''}`}
   120	            onClick={() => handleTabChange('past')}
   121	          >
   122	            Past
   123	          </button>
   124	        </div>
   125	
   126	        {/* Event List */}
   127	        <div className={styles.eventList}>
   128	          {filteredEvents.length === 0 ? (
   129	            <p>No events found for this status.</p>
   130	          ) : (
   131	            filteredEvents.map((event) => (
   132	              <div key={event.id} className={styles.eventCard}>
   133	                <div className={styles.eventDetails}>
   134	                  <div className={styles.eventDateTime}>
   135	                    <p>{event.date}</p>
   136	                    <p>{event.time}</p>
   137	                  </div>
   138	                  <div className={styles.eventInfo}>
   139	                    <p className={styles.eventTitle}>{event.title}</p>
   140	                    <p>{event.participants.join(' and ')}</p>
   141	                  </div>
   142	                </div>
   143	
   144	                {/* Status and Actions */}
   145	                <div className={styles.eventActions}>
   146	                  {event.status === 'pending' ? (
   147	                    <>
   148	                      <button
   149	                        className={styles.participantButton}
   150	                        onClick={() =>
   151	                          setShowParticipants(showParticipants === event.id ? null : event.id)
   152	                        }
   153	                      >
   154	                        Participant ({event.participantList.length})
   155	                      </button>
   156	                      {showParticipants === event.id && (
   157	                        <div className={styles.participantDropdown}>
   158	                          <div className={styles.participantHeader}>
   159	                            <span>Participant ({event.participantList.length})</span>

   183	                            >
   184	                              Reject
   185	                            </button>

   198	                      className={`${styles.statusButton} ${
   199	                        event.status === 'upcoming'
   200	                          ? styles.accepted
   201	                          : event.status === 'cancelled'
   202	                          ? styles.rejected
   203	                          : ''
   204	                      }`}
   205	                    >
   206	                      {event.status === 'upcoming' ? 'Accepted' : 'Rejected'}
   207	                    </button>
   208	                  )}
   209	                  {event.participantCount && (
   210	                    <div className={styles.participantCount}>
   211	                      <span role="img" aria-label="people">
   212	                        👥
   213	                      </span>{' '}
   214	                      {event.participantCount} people
   215	                    </div>
   216	                  )}
   217	                </div>
   218	              </div>
   219	            ))
   220	          )}
   221	        </div>
   222	      </div>

   224	  );

File: ./frontend/src/components/ui/ApprovalButtons.jsx
----------------
     1	// ApprovalButtons.jsx
     2	import React from 'react';
     3	import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
     4	import styles from '../../styles/ApprovalButtons.module.css'; // Create a new CSS file for styles
     5	import crossCircle from '../../assets/icons/crossCircle.svg';
     6	import checkMark from '../../assets/icons/checkMark.svg';
     7	
     8	const ApprovalButtons = ({ onAccept, onReject }) => {
     9	  return (
    10	    <div className={styles.actionButtons}>
    11	      <button className={`${styles.actions} ${styles.rejectButton}`} onClick={onReject}>
    12	        <img src={crossCircle} className="icon" alt="Reject" />
    13	        Reject
    14	      </button>
    15	      <button className={`${styles.actions} ${styles.acceptButton}`} onClick={onAccept}>
    16	        <img src={checkMark} className="icon" alt="Accept" />
    17	        Accept
    18	      </button>
    19	    </div>
    20	  );
    21	};
    22	
    23	ApprovalButtons.propTypes = {
    24	  onAccept: PropTypes.func.isRequired,

File: ./frontend/src/components/ui/ToastContainer.jsx
----------------
     1	import { useState } from 'react';
     2	import Toast from './Toast';
     3	
     4	const ToastContainer = () => {
     5	  const [toasts, setToasts] = useState([]);
     6	
     7	  const addToast = (message, type = 'success', duration = 3000) => {
     8	    const id = Date.now();
     9	    setToasts((prev) => [...prev, { id, message, type, duration }]);
    10	  };
    11	
    12	  const removeToast = (id) => {
    13	    setToasts((prev) => prev.filter((toast) => toast.id !== id));
    14	  };
    15	
    16	  window.addToast = addToast;
    17	
    18	  return (
    19	    <div>
    20	      {toasts.map((toast) => (
    21	        <Toast
    22	          key={toast.id}
    23	          message={toast.message}
    24	          type={toast.type}
    25	          duration={toast.duration}
    26	          onClose={() => removeToast(toast.id)}
    27	        />
    28	      ))}
    29	    </div>
    30	  );
    31	};
    32	
    33	export const showToast = () => window.addToast;
    34	export default ToastContainer;
=================

File: ./frontend/src/components/ui/Toast.jsx
----------------
     1	import { useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import styles from '../../styles/Toast.module.css';
     3	
     4	const Toast = ({ message, type = 'success', duration = 3000, width = 200, onClose }) => {
     5	  useEffect(() => {
     6	    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
     7	      onClose();
     8	    }, duration);
     9	
    10	    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
    11	  }, [duration, onClose]);
    12	
    13	  return (
    14	    <div className={`${styles.toast} ${styles[type]}`}>
    15	      <span className={styles.message} style={{width: `${width}px`}}>{message}</span>
    16	      <button className={styles.closeButton} onClick={onClose}>
    17	        ×
    18	      </button>
    19	    </div>
    20	  );
    21	};
    22	
    23	export default Toast;

File: ./README.md

     1	# Meeting & Event Scheduling Platform
     2	
     3	## Setup Instructions
     4	1. Clone the repository: `git clone <repo-url>`
     5	2. Navigate to backend: `cd backend`
     6	3. Install dependencies: `npm install`
     7	4. Set up environment variables in `.env`:
     8	   - `PORT`: Server port (default: 5000)
     9	   - `MONGO_URI`: MongoDB connection string
    10	   - `JWT_SECRET`: Secret key for JWT
    11	5. Run the server: `npm start`
    12	
    13	## Features
    14	- User signup/login
    15	- Event creation and management
    16	- Availability settings and conflict detection
    17	
    18	## Demo Credentials
    19	- Email: test@example.com
    20	- Password: Test1234
